<review>We bought a brand new Lance 650 truck camper from Lance it did not work for us so I listed it on Craigslist a few days later somebody from Lemke RV called us and said they would have no problem selling this brand new camper luckily I negotiated only leaving it there for 6 months because once they get possession of the camper they listed it for thousands more than you can buy a new one for at Lance I couldn't believe it of course it never sold even though I kept dropping my price six months later I returned to Lemke RV to pick up my camper of course the battery was completely dead even though it had a solar panel on the roof and the inside of this brand new Lance 650 was completely Dusty and full of leaves and debris that blew around there lot I brought it home and had to detail the camper it took me two weeks to sell it on Craigslist so be careful when somebody calls you from Lemke and promising you they can sell your RV then adding thousands of dollars to what your price and then adding tax on top of that.. yeah yeah yeah they have a nice lot and they are well spoken and seemed very friendly but don't let that fool you your RV could stay there for months..... I do not like doing reviews like this but itit's my duty to let the community know what could happen once you sign the contract with Lemke RV    again I'm sorry for leaving such a bad review but it's a true story don't let this happen to you...

Here are a few things I've learned buying RVs
If you buy a truck camper remember you got to climb a flight of stairs to get in and it's hard on dogs 2
If you buy a travel trailer make sure it has two axles 1 axle it's not enough and your travel trailer will bounce and toss your belongings all over not to mention 1 axle is not enough for the weight after it's loaded
If you buy a motorhome or something with a motor remember they sit for a while you will spend lots of money on the motor transmission the exhaust the tires the shocks alternator radiator and a whole lot more that comes with a coach with a motor
I believe the best way to camp is worth a small 20 foot travel trailer with two axles when you're not using it your motors not rotting transmissions not rotting the exhaust is not rusting the starter is not freezing up and the alternator is not going bad
And whatever you do do not buy a Lance camper
Best campers or Winnebago and Jay flight and if you can afford it airstream
Happy camping</review>< pictures>

<gmapID>0x808561130dd2d305:0xf49506bcac8d4d52<//gmapID>< text>
I lived at Villa Montanaro for 2 years, and I‚Äôve never been so sad to move out of a place. I would be living here for a 3rd year if it wasn‚Äôt for job relocation. Here‚Äôs my TL; DR review: the units and amenities are above average, and you get tremendous value for your money by living here.

PROS:
-Units are clean, have big windows that let in lots of light, and have floor plans that make good use of the square footage. To my knowledge, in-unit W/D, ice maker, small patio, and central heat and AC are standard.

-Well-insulated. We rarely turned on the heater during the winter. In the summertime, it can get warm on the top floors, but that‚Äôs what the AC is for!

-The staff here is great, especially Jesse on the maintenance team. One time when our fridge wasn‚Äôt working, he spent over an hour on the weekend fixing it.

-Amazon hub package lockers are amazing.

-Free, unassigned parking in the back lot is plentiful. Or you can pay extra for an assigned carport or space in the garage ($75/mo).

-Great location. Walking distance from BART and next to 680.

-There are luxury apartment buildings in the downtown Walnut Creek area that have nicer amenities (ex: Brio, Lyric), but they are also much more expensive. I feel like VM provided better value for your money.

-You will only hear BART if it‚Äôs a quiet night, and your windows are open. We had also looked at Avalon Walnut Creek and Walnut Ridge, which both had noise concerns.

-In the past 2 years, they have upgrades  like adding package lockers, re-painting the exterior of the complex, replacing the pool furniture, and renovating the clubhouse (not currently open due to COVID)

-Neighbors are friendly and respectful.

-We parked one car in the garage and one on the street/free parking lot and never had any issues w/ crime. However, I‚Äôve seen a ton of smashed car windows at the end of the Coggins Dr closest to BART, where a lot of commuters park before jumping on BART. The section of Coggins in front of VM seems to be OK, but just keep in mind.

-Common areas and landscaping are well-maintained

CONS:
-They are owned by a larger company called Windsor, who increase the rent every year. For our 1 bedroom apt (946 sq. ft.), the rent was $2,665 the 1st year, $2,743 the 2nd year, and would‚Äôve been $2,770 for a 3rd year. I wish that management had shown more of an effort to retain residents, but that being said, it‚Äôs not like rent increases are uncommon, and the increases aren‚Äôt outrageous. But comparatively, Park Regency kept my rent flat for 3 years.

Also when we were negotiating the rent for the 2nd year, one of the former leasing consultants tried to tell me how the new Avalon building down the street would increase rental prices in the area, which irked me. I felt like VM wanted to charge higher prices like Avalon, but Avalon‚Äôs amenities are nicer, and their building is brand new, so it‚Äôs not exactly apples to apples.

-The pricing on the website changes daily. If you have a lot of time before you need to move, I recommend checking the prices every day because I‚Äôve seen the monthly rent on a unit change by like $200 over a 2 week period. And if you see a deal for ‚Äúup to 1 month free,‚Äù call them and double check the deal for a specific unit. When moved in, they were giving 1 month free on 2 br apts but only $500 off 1 br‚Äôs.

-We had a top floor corner unit. On the side of the apartment next to the hallway, you can hear doors closing, people walking past, etc. The side of the apartment next to our neighbors was quieter, which made me wonder if they just skimped on the insulation on the hallway side. I loved how quiet our unit was, but things might be a little more noisy if you‚Äôre not on the top floor.

-Wish the gym was bigger.

-The paint and carpet in the hallways are outdated, but how much time do you really spend in the hallway? I‚Äôd rather have a nice apartment than nice hallways.</text>

< text>
I went to Spreen Acura on a Thursday evening, arriving at 8:20 p.m. It was pretty quiet around the showroom at that time of night. Hunter the Acura Salesman came out of his office and said hello. I told him that I wanted to check out the Acura RDX, which is a SUV version of the four door aging sedan that I am currently driving. He said, "Look no further, you are standing right beside one." He showed me the inside of the showroom model, then he went to the back lot, and reappeared with an Acura RDX that looked just like the one in the showroom. He said, "Get in, and make yourself comfortable." He got in the passenger side, and gave me a nice verbal tour of the features in the cockpit of the RDX. Then we rolled out of the dealership driveway and did circle around the Riverside Auto Center. He had me try the Comfort versus Sport modes, and pointed out a few other features. When we got back to the dealership, he parked the RDX and we chatted awhile longer about the RDX and other non-car related topics. He told me that when I was ready to buy, to come visit him.
The whole experience was friendly and low key. Hunter was not the typical pushy car salesman. It was one of my best car shopping experiences.</text>

< Review>
This is our second experience with Acura of Riverside, and both experiences have been very pleasant. In the first transaction, we traded our RDX for a 2014 MDX. After shopping multiple dealerships for the right deal, the team at Riverside was able to meet our requirements and close the deal at a price that was very acceptable.

In this second transaction, the process was even better. They knew our MDX lease was coming to a close, and they offered to swap our 2014 MDX with a new 2017 MDX at a similar price with no money out of pocket.

After agreeing to a price, color, and features, all we had to do was figure out how to get to the dealer to complete the deal (we now live in San Diego) and all they had to do was find the vehicle configured as we requested. Once the right vehicle was located in Mission Viejo, Jonathan Marquez offered to go above and beyond to help close the deal so that we could receive our new vehicle without having to go to the dealer at all by driving it, along with the paperwork, to our house and exchange vehicles there. This was a remarkable service by Jonathan and he was very good about communication and timing so that we could plan for his arrival.

Once at our house, we completed the paperwork and a review of the new features of the new MDX within about 45 minutes.

We are delighted and would recommend Acura of Riverside to anyone who asks.

Thank you Jonathan, and your support team for making this happen so smoothly.< /Review>
